<div style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;"><b>Item 2.02 Results of Operations and Financial Condition</b></div>

<div style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -9pt;">&#xa0;</div>

<div style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;">On&#xa0;August 14, 2023,&#xa0; ParkerVision, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) issued a press release which reported financial and operating results for the three and six months ended June 30, 2023. A copy of the press release is attached as Exhibit 99.1 and is incorporated herein by reference.</div>

<div style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -9pt;">&#xa0;</div>

<div style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;">The information contained in this Current Report on Form 8-K, including Exhibit 99.1 hereto, has been &#8220;furnished&#8221; and shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section 18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, or otherwise subject to liability under that section. The information in this Current Report shall not be incorporated by reference into any filing or other document pursuant to the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such filing or document.</div>

<div style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -9pt;">&#xa0;</div>

<body style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; padding: 0in 0.1in; cursor: auto;">
<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: right; font-size: 11pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif;"><font style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 11pt;"><b>&nbsp;Exhibit 99.1</b></font></p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: left; font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif;"><font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 14pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: center; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;"><b>ParkerVision Reports Profitable First Half of <a data-tblloc="0x1" data-tblname="384391" data-tblv="7" id="led384391F20232231679594586844">2023</a> </b></p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;"><b>JACKSONVILLE</b><b>, Fla.,&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="21x1" data-tblname="384392" data-tblv="7" id="led384392F20232231679594614065">August 14, 2023</a> </b>&#8211;<b> </b>ParkerVision, Inc. (OTCQB: PRKR) (&#8220;ParkerVision&#8221; or the "Company"), a developer and marketer of technologies and products for wireless applications, today announced results for the three and <a data-tblloc="13x1" data-tblname="384392" data-tblv="7" id="led384392F20232231679594637533">six months ended June 30, 2023</a>.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;"><b><i>First Half&nbsp; <a data-tblloc="0x1" data-tblname="384391" data-tblv="7" id="led384391F20232231679594669899">2023</a>&nbsp;Summary and Recent Developments</i></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 36pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">The Company recognized $25 million in revenue from patent license and settlement agreements and, after recognizing contingent legal fees and expenses, reported net income of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x5" data-tblname="384395" data-tblv="7" id="led384395F2023731691091572861">$14.5</a> million in the first half of 2023.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 36pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; margin: 0pt;">The Company recently filed patent infringement cases in the Western District of Texas against Texas Instruments and NXP Semiconductors and additional cases against Taiwanese chip companies MediaTek and Realtek.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 36pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; margin: 0pt;">During the second quarter of 2023, the Company received $5 million in new funding under its contingent payment agreement.&nbsp;</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 36pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">The Company continues to await its hearing date in the appeal of its patent infringement case against Qualcomm in the Middle District of Florida.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;">Jeffrey Parker, Chairman and Chief Executive Officer, commented, &#8220;ParkerVision currently has a dozen open cases in U.S. Federal Courts against eight companies to enforce our patent rights for the unauthorized use of our wireless technologies. We strongly believe the innovations covered by ParkerVision's patents have enabled more competitive and compelling wireless products, and we encourage those who have benefited from incorporating our technology into their products to obtain authorization to use our protected intellectual property through a license.&nbsp; As we learn of additional infringement, we expect to continue to expand the enforcement of our patent rights."</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;">Mr. Parker continued, &#8220;ParkerVision has invested hundreds of millions of dollars in R&amp;D and marketing in its patented RF receiver and transmitter technologies to enable ultra-small semiconductor chips that deliver high-performance RF wireless communications for mobile telephone standards such as 3G, 4G, and 5G, Wi-Fi&#174; communications, Bluetooth&#174;, satellite communications and other wireless applications.&#8221;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-variant:normal;text-align:center;margin:0pt;">&#65279;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;"><b><i>Financial Results</i></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 43px;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 21px;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: 1417px;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">ParkerVision reported net income for the second quarter of <a data-tblloc="0x1" data-tblname="384391" data-tblv="7" id="led384391F20232231679594889334">2023</a> of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="384395" data-tblv="7" id="led384395F2023731691091798320">$1.4</a> million, or&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="384395" data-tblv="7" id="led384395F2023731691091818046">$0.02</a> per common share, compared to a net loss of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x2" data-tblname="384395" data-tblv="7" id="led384395F2023731691091853031">($4.4)</a> million, or&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x2" data-tblname="384395" data-tblv="7" id="led384395F2023731691091908522">($0.06)</a> per common share for the second quarter of <a data-tblloc="32x1" data-tblname="384391" data-tblv="7" id="led384391F20232231679594923115">2022</a>.&nbsp; The increase in net income is largely a result of a decrease in the estimated fair value of contingent payment obligations.&nbsp;</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt;">

			<td style="vertical-align: top; width: 23px; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; font-size: 11pt; width: 1681px;">
			<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">ParkerVision reported net income for the first half of 2023 of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x5" data-tblname="384395" data-tblv="7" id="led384395F2023731691092851923">$14.5</a> million, or&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x5" data-tblname="384395" data-tblv="7" id="led384395F2023731691092876837">$0.17</a> per common share, compared to a net loss of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x6" data-tblname="384395" data-tblv="7" id="led384395F2023731691092914603">($4.1)</a> million, or&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x6" data-tblname="384395" data-tblv="7" id="led384395F2023731691092959844">$ (0.05)</a> per common share for the second half of 2022.&nbsp;&nbsp; The increase in net income is primarily the result of $25 million in revenue recognized on a patent license and settlement agreement reached in February 2023, offset by contingent legal fees and expenses incurred related to the agreement.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>About ParkerVision</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt;">ParkerVision, Inc. invents, develops and licenses cutting-edge, proprietary radio-frequency (RF) technologies that enable wireless solution providers to make and sell advanced wireless communication products. &nbsp;ParkerVision is engaged in a number of patent enforcement actions in the U.S. to protect patented rights that it believes are broadly infringed by others. For more information, please visit www.parkervision.com.<i> (PRKR-I)</i></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>
